ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent


def test_package_json_declares_node_20_plus() -> None:
    package_json = json.loads((ROOT / "package.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    engines = package_json.get("engines", {})

**Designing active tab scroll behavior**
codex
I’m now editing `assets/js/directory_verified.js` to add a narrow click-path: if the clicked tab is already active and tabs are currently sticky, it will smooth-scroll to `top: 0`; otherwise existing tab activation behavior stays unchanged. Then I’ll add a matching compatibility assertion in `tests/test_frontend_compat.py`.

-      window.activateTab(e.currentTarget);
